 (function() {

  var urls        = [
          '//cdn1.espn.net/fitt/354defedb64e-release-12-19-2018.1/client/espn-en.js',
          '//cdn1.espn.net/fitt/354defedb64e-release-12-19-2018.1/client/schedule.js'
      ],
      urlsToLoad  = [].concat(urls),
      fittHTTP    = null,
      logMetrics  = false,
      startUpAt   = (new Date()).getTime();

  function loadNextURL() {
      var nextURL     = (urlsToLoad.length) ? urlsToLoad.shift() : '';

      if (nextURL) {
          fittHTTP.script(nextURL).then(loadNextURL);
      } else if (urlsToLoad.length) {
          loadNextURL();
      } else if (logMetrics) {
          console.log('All done at (' + urls.length + '): ' + ((new Date()).getTime() - startUpAt));
      }
  }

  function bootstrap() {
      fittHTTP    = (typeof fitt != 'undefined') ? fitt.http : null;

      if (fittHTTP && typeof fittHTTP.script == 'function') {
          if (logMetrics) { console.log('Main ready at: ' + ((new Date()).getTime() - startUpAt)); }
          loadNextURL();
      } else {
          setTimeout(bootstrap, 10);
      }
  }

  bootstrap();
})();
</script>
